### 48 分选日志 Findings So Far
Key files:
- UI/form:
  - `E:\new\48\RSS\Forms\sortlogform.cpp`
  - `E:\new\48\RSS\Forms\sortlogform.h`
  - `E:\new\48\RSS\Forms\sortlogform.ui`
  - style: `E:\new\48\RSS\Forms\qrc\qss\SortLog.qss`
- DB/API client:
  - `E:\new\48\RSS\Base\databaseoperation.cpp`
  - `E:\new\48\RSS\Base\databaseoperation.h`
- Data model:
  - `E:\new\48\RDP_Entity\tb_runningtimeinfo.h`
  - fields:
    ```cpp
    int ID
    QString RunningDate
    QString StartTime
    QString StopTime
    ```
- Global flag:
  - `E:\new\48\RSS\Base\globaldatainterface.h`: `static bool usedSeparationLogFlags`
  - default in `globaldatainterface.cpp`: `true`

### 48 分选日志 Data Source
`SortLogForm::DrawSeparationRunningTimeChart(beginDate, endDate)`:
- Queries date list:
  ```cpp
  GlobalDataInterface::dataBaseOperation.RunningDate(beginDate, endDate)
  ```
- Then for each `RunningDate`, queries detail intervals:
  ```cpp
  GlobalDataInterface::dataBaseOperation.GetRunningTimeInfo(runningDate)
  ```
- Draws per-day 24h chart with QCustomPlot.
- Calculates daily minutes:
  ```cpp
  TodayMinutes[i] += StartTime.secsTo(StopTime)/60
  ```
- Shows total accumulated minutes.
- Date range limit: max 31 days; otherwise warning `30001103`.

DB/API methods in `databaseoperation.cpp`:
- `InsertRunningStopTime(runningDate, startTime, stopTime)`
  - API: `Api/FruitInfo/SaveRunningTimeInfoByStopTime`
- `GetRunningTimeInfoByStopTime(stopTime)`
  - API: `Api/FruitInfo/GetRunningTimeInfo`
  - used with empty string `""` to find unfinished interval.
- `UpdateRunningStopTime(tb_RunningTimeInfo*)`
  - same save API.
- `RunningDate(beginDate, endDate)`
  - API: `Api/FruitInfo/GetRunningTimeInfoByRunningDate`
- `GetRunningTimeInfo(runningDate)`
  - API: `Api/FruitInfo/GetRunningTimeInfo`

Likely underlying table name: `tb_RunningTimeInfo` / similar casing, inferred from model/entity and API names. 48 client does not directly show SQL table for this API.

### What Writes 分选日志
Main write logic is in `E:\new\48\RSS\Forms\homeform.cpp`.

1. Startup cleanup:
   - `HomeForm` constructor:
     ```cpp
     if (GlobalDataInterface::usedSeparationLogFlags) {
         CheckRunningTime();
     }
     ```
   - `CheckRunningTime()`:
     - Calls `GetRunningTimeInfo("")`.
     - For any records, sets `StopTime = item->StartTime`.
     - Resets `RunningTimeInfoStopTimeIsEmptyFlags = false`.
     - This closes stale/unclosed records from previous run.

2. Regular runtime loop, around `homeform.cpp` lines ~2444:
   - Every ~30 seconds:
     - If `usedSeparationLogFlags`.
     - Uses `lVelChangelabelValue` (machine speed) to detect running/stopped.
   - If speed > 0 and no open interval:
     ```cpp
     InsertRunningStopTime(today, currentTime, "")
     RunningTimeInfoStopTimeIsEmptyFlags = true
     ```
   - If `isEndProcess` or speed == 0 and there is open interval:
     ```cpp
     GetRunningTimeInfoByStopTime("")
     StopTime = current time
     UpdateRunningStopTime(...)
     isEndProcess = false
     RunningTimeInfoStopTimeIsEmptyFlags = false
     ```
   - Cross-midnight:
     - If current open record date != today, time is `00:00`, speed > 0:
       - Stop old record at `23:59:59`.
       - Sets flag false, then new record can be inserted for new day.

3. HomeForm init/load area around lines ~192:
   - Gets open running record with `GetRunningTimeInfoByStopTime("")`.
   - If same date: set StopTime to current time.
   - Else: set StopTime to `23:59:59`.
   - This appears to close unfinished open intervals when home form initializes.

4. App exit / display off in `mainform.cpp` around ~1700 and ~1732:
   - If `usedSeparationLogFlags`, finds open interval and sets StopTime to current time.

5. Language switch:
   - `languageswitchform.cpp` around ~148 does same close-open-interval logic.

6. `WriteProcessLog()` is not 分选日志 data source:
   - Despite name, it logs fruit/grade/export process SQL-ish info when ending process or loading config. It is not used by `SortLogForm`.

### Current Harmony State Relevant to 分选日志
- Harmony currently has a `MoreContent.openSortLogDialog()` and UI state:
  - `showSortLogDialog`
  - `sortLogStartDate`
  - `sortLogEndDate`
  - `sortLogItems`
- Existing Harmony implementation may be local/hardcoded or incomplete. Need inspect before changing.
- Backend may already have running-time APIs? Need search in `E:\goTest` for `RunningTimeInfo`, `running_time`, `FruitInfo`, etc.
- User expects backend Go to query DB and return data to frontend; frontend should not do complex data processing.

### Recommended Next Steps
1. Explain findings to user briefly in Chinese:
   - 48 分选日志来源是 `tb_RunningTimeInfo` via `Api/FruitInfo/...`.
   - It records machine running intervals based on speed > 0 and stop/end/exit events.
   - UI queries by date range and renders per-day intervals and accumulated minutes.
2. If user asks to implement:
   - Inspect Go backend DB schema and APIs for running time info.
   - If missing, add Go API/WebSocket topic for:
     - Query running dates by date range.
     - Query intervals by running date, or return grouped result in one call.
     - Optionally record/close running intervals if backend should manage it.
   - Inspect Harmony `MoreContent.openSortLogDialog()` and replace with backend API call.
   - Keep frontend display simple: date range, list/chart-like intervals, daily total, total minutes.
3. Do not commit unless user explicitly asks.

---


**OpenAI Codex**

看完了，48 的“分选日志”确实是从数据库/本地服务拿的，不是前端自己算出来的。

核心数据源是 `tb_RunningTimeInfo`：

[sortlogform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/sortlogform.cpp:99) 里 `DrawSeparationRunningTimeChart()` 会：

1. 先按日期范围查有哪些运行日期  
   `RunningDate(beginDate, endDate)`  
   对应接口：`Api/FruitInfo/GetRunningTimeInfoByRunningDate`

2. 再按每天查运行时间段  
   `GetRunningTimeInfo(runningDate)`  
   对应接口：`Api/FruitInfo/GetRunningTimeInfo`

结构体在 [tb_runningtimeinfo.h](E:/new/48/RDP_Entity/tb_runningtimeinfo.h:7)：

```cpp
ID
RunningDate
StartTime
StopTime
```

写入数据库的地方主要在首页运行逻辑：

[homeform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/homeform.cpp:2441) 每 30 秒检查一次分选速度 `lVelChangelabelValue`：

- 速度 `> 0`，并且当前没有未关闭记录：插入一条运行开始记录，`StopTime=""`
- 速度 `== 0` 或者 `isEndProcess`：查出 `StopTime=""` 的记录，把 `StopTime` 更新成当前时间
- 跨天时：旧日期记录会被结束到 `23:59:59`

对应数据库接口在 [databaseoperation.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Base/databaseoperation.cpp:845)：

```cpp
InsertRunningStopTime(...)
UpdateRunningStopTime(...)
RunningDate(...)
GetRunningTimeInfo(...)
GetRunningTimeInfoByStopTime("")
```

另外，分选日志双击某一天会打开“分选效率图”，这个是另一份数据：`tb_SeparationEfficiencyInfo`。在机器运行时，48 每隔一段时间写一次分选效率：

[homeform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/homeform.cpp:2487)  
接口是 `Api/FruitInfo/SaveSeparationEfficiencyInfo`，查询是 `Api/FruitInfo/GetSeparationEfficiencyInfo`。

所以如果我们鸿蒙要照 48 做，正确方向是：前端只传开始日期、结束日期给 Go，Go 后端查询 `tb_RunningTimeInfo`，整理成每天的运行区间和累计分钟数返回；前端只负责显示。分选效率图如果也要做，再单独加 `tb_SeparationEfficiencyInfo` 的查询。

**OpenAI Codex**

对，48 中文资源里叫 **分选日志**，英文标题才是 **Sorting Log / SortLog**。

它里面确实是“图”，不是普通表格列表。48 用的是 `QCustomPlot` 画一条 24 小时横向时间轴：

- 每一天一行图
- X 轴是 `00:00` 到 `24:00`
- 有运行的时间段用青绿色块/线填出来
- 右边显示当天累计分钟数
- 底部还有总累计分钟数
- 双击某一天的图，会打开“分选效率图”

所以它本质是“运行时间段图表”。我刚才鸿蒙这边做的是用 ArkUI 画了一个类似的时间条，不是完整图表库版，但视觉和数据结构是照 48 的方向来的。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

现在鸿蒙/Go 这边我只实现了 **读取 `tb_RunningTimeInfo` 显示分选日志**，还没有实现写入。

48 里写入的是这几个字段：

```text
ID
RunningDate
StartTime
StopTime
```

写入规则是：

- 机器开始分选：速度 `lVelChangelabelValue > 0`
  - 插入一条记录：
  ```text
  RunningDate = 当前日期
  StartTime = 当前时间
  StopTime = ""
  ```

- 机器停止分选：速度 `== 0` 或结束分选 `isEndProcess`
  - 查 `StopTime == ""` 的当前未关闭记录
  - 更新：
  ```text
  StopTime = 当前时间
  ```

- 跨天：
  - 旧记录更新：
  ```text
  StopTime = "23:59:59"
  ```
  - 新的一天如果还在运行，再插入新记录

- 启动/退出/切换语言时：
  - 如果发现 `StopTime == ""` 的未关闭记录，会补一个结束时间，避免日志一直开着。

48 写入入口主要在 `homeform.cpp`，数据库接口是：

```cpp
InsertRunningStopTime(runningDate, startTime, stopTime)
UpdateRunningStopTime(tb_RunningTimeInfo*)
GetRunningTimeInfoByStopTime("")
```

所以我们 Go 这边下一步要补的是：在后端根据实时分选速度/结束分选事件，自动插入和关闭 `tb_RunningTimeInfo`。当前只有查询展示，还没写库。

看到关键点了：写入不是按水果明细写，而是按“机器有速度/停止”记录一段运行区间。还剩 mainform 那几个退出/切换场景，我补一下行号。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

不是每颗水果写一条。`tb_RunningTimeInfo` 记录的是“分选运行时间段”。

48 里面写入点主要在这里：

[databaseoperation.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Base/databaseoperation.cpp:845)  
`InsertRunningStopTime(runningDate, startTime, stopTime)` 和 `UpdateRunningStopTime(...)` 都调用：

```text
Api/FruitInfo/SaveRunningTimeInfoByStopTime
```

写入字段就是：

```text
ID
RunningDate  // yyyy-MM-dd
StartTime    // hh:mm:ss
StopTime     // hh:mm:ss，运行中先写空字符串
```

触发条件在 [homeform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/homeform.cpp:2444)：

1. 必须开启 `GlobalDataInterface::usedSeparationLogFlags`，默认是 true：  
   [globaldatainterface.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Base/globaldatainterface.cpp:95)

2. 每隔 30 秒检查一次。

3. 如果当前分选速度 `lVelChangelabelValue > 0`，并且没有未结束记录，就插入一条：

```cpp
InsertRunningStopTime(今天日期, 当前时间, "")
```

对应 [homeform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/homeform.cpp:2461)。

4. 如果 `isEndProcess == true` 或速度变成 `0`，并且当前有未结束记录，就把这条记录的 `StopTime` 更新成当前时间：  
[homeform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/homeform.cpp:2469)

5. 如果跨天了，旧记录会被补成 `23:59:59`：  
[homeform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/homeform.cpp:2450)

还有一些兜底关闭场景：
- 启动时发现有 `StopTime=""` 的旧记录，会补 StopTime： [homeform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/homeform.cpp:192)
- 切换语言时会关闭未结束记录： [languageswitchform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/languageswitchform.cpp:148)
- mainform 某些退出/停止流程也会关闭未结束记录： [mainform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/mainform.cpp:1702)

我们现在 Go 这边目前只有读，没有写：  
[go/running_time_info_api.go](E:/goTest/go/ohos/database/running_time_info_api.go:37) 只注册了 `/Api/FruitInfo/GetSortLog` 查询接口。

所以如果你现在鸿蒙分选日志没数据，很正常：Go 后端还没有实现 48 那套“速度大于 0 插入、速度为 0/结束时更新 StopTime”的写入逻辑。

**OpenAI Codex**

对，你的鸿蒙现在没有真正写入 `tb_RunningTimeInfo` 的逻辑。

我刚扫了两边：

- 鸿蒙前端现在只查：`LocalWebApiClient.getSortLog()` 调 `/Api/FruitInfo/GetSortLog`
- Go 后端现在也只读：`QuerySortLog()` 从 `tb_RunningTimeInfo` 查数据
- `NoDatabaseServices.ets` 里虽然有 `insert()`、`updateStopTime()` 这些名字，但都是占位：

```ts
void runningDate
void startTime
void stopTime
return Date.now()
```

也就是说：它不会发 API，不会写 SQLite，不会写 Go 后端数据库。

所以当前状态是：分选日志 UI 和查询接口有了，但数据来源表 `tb_RunningTimeInfo` 没有人写。  
如果要按 48 实现，应该在 Go 后端做运行状态检测和写库：速度 > 0 时插入 `StartTime`，速度归 0 或结束分选时更新 `StopTime`。前端最多只是显示，不处理这个业务逻辑。

**User**

那这个和历史加工保存数据有什么区别吗？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

有区别，两个表/功能不是一回事：

`tb_RunningTimeInfo` 是“分选运行时间段日志”。  
它只关心机器什么时候开始跑、什么时候停，用来画你现在这个“分选日志”的时间条。字段很少：`RunningDate / StartTime / StopTime`。比如 09:10 开始有速度，09:30 停了，就记录一段 `09:10:11 - 09:30:00`。

历史加工保存数据更像“批次加工结果/历史报表数据”。  
它保存的是这批水果的统计结果、客户、农场、品种、批次号、总个数、总重量、等级、出口、开始结束时间等，用来历史查询、报表、结束分选后的汇总。它是业务结果数据。

简单说：

- 分选日志：记录“设备什么时候在跑”
- 历史加工：记录“这批货加工出了什么结果”

它们会发生在同一次加工过程中，但用途不同。  
分选日志按速度状态自动开段/闭段；历史加工一般在实时保存、结束分选、批次保存时写入。

---


**User**

**OpenAI Codex**

**OpenAI Codex**

**OpenAI Codex**

修好了，问题就在这一段：

[HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/utils/network/HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets:2008)

`catch((error) => ...)` 里的 `error` 被 ArkTS 推成了禁用类型，所以编译报 `arkts-no-any-unknown`。我改成了显式类型：

```ts
.catch((error: Error | BusinessError | Object | string): void => {
  const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
  ...
})
```

我做了 `git diff --check`，没发现格式问题。没有跑 hvigor，你再编译一下看看。

**OpenAI Codex**

我看懂了，你这个截图里最大的问题是“图表显示区被压到下面去了”，中间一大块空白；48 的分选日志图应该从查询栏下面开始显示，不应该贴近底部。我先对照 48 的 `sortlogform` 和现在的 `SortLogDialog`，然后直接改显示布局。

**OpenAI Codex**

48 里是 `QCustomPlot`，每一天一个 130px 左右的图，图从显示面板顶部往下排；右侧是“累计 xx 分钟”，底部再放 Total。你现在不是数据错，是 Scroll/Column 的高度分配让图跑到底部了。

You are a deeply pragmatic, effective software engineer. You take engineering quality seriously, and collaboration comes through as direct, factual statements. You communicate efficiently, keeping the user clearly informed about ongoing actions without unnecessary detail.

## Values
You are guided by these core values:

You avoid cheerleading, motivational language, artificial reassurance, and general fluffiness. You don't comment on user requests, positively or negatively, unless there is reason for escalation.

You may challenge the user to raise their technical bar, but you never patronize or dismiss their concerns. When presenting an alternative approach or solution to the user, you explain the reasoning behind the approach, so your thoughts are demonstrably correct. **OpenAI Codex**

我确认了 48 的“下载配置”：

- UI：标题 `DownLoad Config`，表格三列 `File / Type / Date`，底部 `Download / Delete`
- 列表：调用 `Customer/GetDeviceConfig`
- 过滤后缀：`.cmc`、`.rjs`、`.ejs`、`.exp`
- 类型判断：`.exp` / `.ejs` 是工程配置，`.cmc` / `.rjs` 是用户配置
- 下载：调用 `Customer/DownDeviceConfig`，返回 base64，解码后保存到 `config/<VERSION_SHOW>/文件名`
- 删除：调用 `Customer/DeleteDeviceConfig`，成功后本地也删除同名文件，并从表格移除
- 现在鸿蒙旧的 `DownloadConfigDialog.ets` 是“配置快照导出/回读”，可以删掉重做

我建议按这个实现：

- 前端只保留 UI 和按钮事件，不处理 base64、不拼远端签名、不写业务规则。
- Go 后端新增 3 个本地 API：
  - `ListDeviceConfigs`
  - `DownloadDeviceConfig`
  - `DeleteDeviceConfig`
- Go 后端负责：
  - 读取远端 API 地址和 `SecretKey`
  - 按 48 的 AES/MD5 签名规则请求云端
  - 过滤配置文件类型
  - 下载后保存到本机配置目录
  - 删除云端配置并清理本地文件
- 鸿蒙删掉旧 `DownloadConfigDialog.ets` 内容，重做成你图里这种表格弹窗。

需要你确认一个点：Go 后端的远端 API 凭证是否继续从数据库 `tb_sys_configs` 的 `SecretKey` 取？如果是，我就按 48 的逻辑直接实现。

**OpenAI Codex**

48 的加密文件不在 `RSS` 目录本体，可能是工程外部 include。先用现有线索实现兼容版本：AES 加密返回 base64，签名串按 48 的 `data{加密后data}timestamp{毫秒}` 做 MD5 后再 AES。后面如果云端返回签名错误，再调整 AES 模式。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

找到了，48 实际引用的是 `RDP_Common/Encrypt`。我会按这个准确实现，不用猜。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

48 的加密细节确认：AES-256-ECB，key 用 SecretKey UTF-8 后面补空格到 32 字节，PKCS padding，结果 base64；MD5 是小写 hex。这个可以在 Go 里直接复刻。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

保存目录我按 48 的格式保留为 `config/<VERSION_SHOW>/`。Go 里没有 `VERSION_SHOW` 常量，所以会优先从 `tb_sys_configs` 读 `VERSION_SHOW` / `VersionShow` / `软件版本`，都没有就用 `V4.02.01` 兜底。文件目录放在当前数据库文件同级，便于后续恢复配置复用。

后端 Go：
- 新增云端配置接口封装：[device_config_cloud_api.go](E:/goTest/go/ohos/database/device_config_cloud_api.go:1)
- 路由：
  - `/Api/DeviceConfig/GetDeviceConfig`
  - `/Api/DeviceConfig/DownDeviceConfig`
  - `/Api/DeviceConfig/DeleteDeviceConfig`
- Go 负责读取 `tb_sys_configs.SecretKey`，按 48 的 AES-256-ECB + MD5 签名规则请求云端。

- 下载后保存到数据库同级目录：`config/<VERSION_SHOW>/文件名`。
- 如果没有 `SecretKey`，接口会返回错误，前端会提示。

- 旧的快照导出/导入弹窗已替换成 48 风格表格：[DownloadConfigDialog.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/DownloadConfigDialog.ets:1)

**OpenAI Codex**

定位到了，就是 `LocalWebApiClient.post(..., {})`。我改成显式请求类实例，序列化结果仍然是 `{}`。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

改完了。现在做静态检查，确认没有其它裸 `{}` 请求写法。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

已修。

问题点在 [LocalWebApiClient.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/protocol/LocalWebApiClient.ets:133)：

```ts
LocalWebApiClient.post('/Api/DeviceConfig/GetDeviceConfig', {})
```

ArkTS 不允许这种裸对象字面量。我改成了显式类：

```ts
export class DeviceConfigListRequestModel {
}
```

然后调用：

```ts
new DeviceConfigListRequestModel()
```

序列化出来仍然是 `{}`，但符合 ArkTS 规则。

我做了静态检查，没有发现其它 `post(..., {})` 残留；没跑 hvigor。

Continuation behavior:
- This goal persists across turns. Ending this turn does not require shrinking the objective to what fits now.
- Keep the full objective intact. If it cannot be finished now, make concrete progress toward the real requested end state, leave the goal active, and do not redefine success around a smaller or easier task.
- Temporary rough edges are acceptable while the work is moving in the right direction. Completion still requires the requested end state to be true and verified.

Budget:
- Tokens used: 0
- Token budget: none
- Tokens remaining: unbounded

Work from evidence:
Use the current worktree and external state as authoritative. Previous conversation context can help locate relevant work, but inspect the current state before relying on it. Improve, replace, or remove existing work as needed to satisfy the actual objective.

Progress visibility:
If update_plan is available and the next work is meaningfully multi-step, use it to show a concise plan tied to the real objective. Keep the plan current as steps complete or the next best action changes. Skip planning overhead for trivial one-step progress, and do not treat a plan update as a substitute for doing the work.

Fidelity:
- Optimize each turn for movement toward the requested end state, not for the smallest stable-looking subset or easiest passing change.
- Do not substitute a narrower, safer, smaller, merely compatible, or easier-to-test solution because it is more likely to pass current tests.
- Treat alignment as movement toward the requested end state. An edit is aligned only if it makes the requested final state more true; useful-looking behavior that preserves a different end state is misaligned.

Completion audit:
Before deciding that the goal is achieved, treat completion as unproven and verify it against the actual current state:
- Derive concrete requirements from the objective and any referenced files, plans, specifications, issues, or user instructions.
- Preserve the original scope; do not redefine success around the work that already exists.
- For every explicit requirement, numbered item, named artifact, command, test, gate, invariant, and deliverable, identify the authoritative evidence that would prove it, then inspect the relevant current-state sources: files, command output, test results, PR state, rendered artifacts, runtime behavior, or other authoritative evidence.
- For each item, determine whether the evidence proves completion, contradicts completion, shows incomplete work, is too weak or indirect to verify completion, or is missing.
- Match the verification scope to the requirement's scope; do not use a narrow check to support a broad claim.
- Treat tests, manifests, verifiers, green checks, and search results as evidence only after confirming they cover the relevant requirement.
- Treat uncertain or indirect evidence as not achieved; gather stronger evidence or continue the work.
- The audit must prove completion, not merely fail to find obvious remaining work.

Do not rely on intent, partial progress, memory of earlier work, or a plausible final answer as proof of completion. Marking the goal complete is a claim that the full objective has been finished and can withstand requirement-by-requirement scrutiny. Only mark the goal achieved when current evidence proves every requirement has been satisfied and no required work remains. If the evidence is incomplete, weak, indirect, merely consistent with completion, or leaves any requirement missing, incomplete, or unverified, keep working instead of marking the goal complete. If the objective is achieved, call update_goal with status "complete" so usage accounting is preserved. If the achieved goal has a token budget, report the final consumed token budget to the user after update_goal succeeds.

Blocked audit:
- Do not call update_goal with status "blocked" the first time a blocker appears.
- Only use status "blocked" when the same blocking condition has repeated for at least three consecutive goal turns, counting the original/user-triggered turn and any automatic goal continuations.
- If the user resumes a goal that was previously marked "blocked", treat the resumed run as a fresh blocked audit. If the same blocking condition then repeats for at least three consecutive resumed goal turns, call update_goal with status "blocked" again.
- Use status "blocked" only when you are truly at an impasse and cannot make meaningful progress without user input or an external-state change.
- Once the blocked threshold is satisfied, do not keep reporting that you are still blocked while leaving the goal active; call update_goal with status "blocked".
- Never use status "blocked" merely because the work is hard, slow, uncertain, incomplete, or would benefit from clarification.

Do not call update_goal unless the goal is complete or the strict blocked audit above is satisfied. Do not mark a goal complete merely because the budget is nearly exhausted or because you are stopping work.

</codex_internal_context>

**OpenAI Codex**

已看完第一轮关键代码和你发的 UI 图，设计如下：

1. **电气故障设置**
   - 48：`ElectricFaultInfoForm(FType=1)`，读写 `tb_Base_Fault`，UI 只显示 `Code / Module / Message`，底部 `Import / Save`。
   - 鸿蒙：删掉当前本地假数据 UI，改成同款暗色表格。
   - 后端 Go：新增 `/Api/Fault/GetListBaseFaultInfo`、`/Api/Fault/SaveBaseFaults`、`/Api/Fault/DeleteBaseFaultInfo`，直接操作 `tb_Base_Fault`。
   - 前端只调用 API，不再自己处理/持久化故障数据。

2. **故障信息**
   - 48：查询 `tb_FaultInfo`，默认最近一个月，列为 `Category / Code / Module / Message / Status / Start Time / End Time`，底部时间范围 + Information + Query。
   - 鸿蒙：按你图里的 UI 重做，数据从 Go API 查询。
   - Go：新增故障信息查询接口，按开始时间、结束时间、关键字过滤。

3. **打印设置 + 打印预览**
   - 48：打印模板设置保存顶部字段勾选、内容字段勾选、列宽；打印预览按模板决定显示哪些字段。
   - 鸿蒙：当前 JSON 打印配置保留数据模型但 UI 改成 48 样式；预览组件读取同一份配置，字段隐藏和列宽同步生效。
   - 这个主要是前端功能，除非发现需要后端保存 `PrintSetName`，否则不动 Go。

4. **检查新版本**
   - 48：显示 RSS/FSM/WAM 三块版本，版本来自本地/下位机版本 + 云端更新信息；按钮目前用于更新。
   - 鸿蒙：先按你的要求“主要看下位机传输内容然后显示”，实现 RSS/FSM/WAM 当前版本展示；云端更新可先接 Go API 查询，按钮保留但不做危险更新动作，避免误触升级。
   - Go：需要提供当前版本汇总接口，必要时代理云端版本接口。

5. **设备信息**
   - 48：设备编号、客户、地址、版本信息、到期时间等；部分来自云端客户设备信息，部分来自本地下位机版本/配置。
   - 鸿蒙：删当前本地 storage UI，改成图里的 48 样式；前端展示和提交给 Go，Go 负责读写本地配置/云端交互。
   - 版本字段优先用当前已收到的下位机版本数据。

- 前端仓库干净。
- 后端只有 `.waylog/history` 未提交无关文件，我不会碰。
- 需要你确认：**我就按上面方案开始实现**。确认后我从“电气故障设置”开始，完成一个功能就提交一个 commit。

**OpenAI Codex**

<permissions instructions>
Filesystem sandboxing defines which files can be read or written. `sandbox_mode` is `workspace-write`: The sandbox permits reading files, and editing files in `cwd` and `writable_roots`. Editing files in other directories requires approval. Network access is restricted.
# Escalation Requests

Commands are run outside the sandbox if they are approved by the user, or match an existing rule that allows it to run unrestricted. The command string is split into independent command segments at shell control operators, including but not limited to:

- Pipes: |
- Logical operators: &&, ||
- Command separators: ;
- Subshell boundaries: (...), $(...)

Each resulting segment is evaluated independently for sandbox restrictions and approval requirements.

Example:

git pull | tee output.txt

This is treated as two command segments:

["git", "pull"]

["tee", "output.txt"]

Commands that use more advanced shell features like redirection (>, >>, <), substitutions ($(...), ...), environment variables (FOO=bar), or wildcard patterns (*, ?) will not be evaluated against rules, to limit the scope of what an approved rule allows.

## How to request escalation

IMPORTANT: To request approval to execute a command that will require escalated privileges:

- Provide the `sandbox_permissions` parameter with the value `"require_escalated"`
- Include a short question asking the user if they want to allow the action in `justification` parameter. e.g. "Do you want to download and install dependencies for this project?"
- Optionally suggest a `prefix_rule` - this will be shown to the user with an option to persist the rule approval for future sessions.

If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with "require_escalated". ALWAYS proceed to use the `justification` parameter - do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.

## When to request escalation

While commands are running inside the sandbox, here are some scenarios that will require escalation outside the sandbox:

- You need to run a command that writes to a directory that requires it (e.g. running tests that write to /var)
- You need to run a GUI app (e.g., open/xdg-open/osascript) to open browsers or files.
- If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with `require_escalated`. ALWAYS proceed to use the `sandbox_permissions` and `justification` parameters. do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.
- You are about to take a potentially destructive action such as an `rm` or `git reset` that the user did not explicitly ask for.
- Be judicious with escalating, but if completing the user's request requires it, you should do so - don't try and circumvent approvals by using other tools.

## prefix_rule guidance

When choosing a `prefix_rule`, request one that will allow you to fulfill similar requests from the user in the future without re-requesting escalation. It should be categorical and reasonably scoped to similar capabilities. You should rarely pass the entire command into `prefix_rule`.

### Banned prefix_rules 
Avoid requesting overly broad prefixes that the user would be ill-advised to approve. For example, do not request ["python3"], ["python", "-"], or other similar prefixes that would allow arbitrary scripting.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule argument for destructive commands like rm.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule if your command uses a heredoc or herestring. 

### Examples
Good examples of prefixes:
- ["npm", "run", "dev"]
- ["gh", "pr", "check"]
- ["cargo", "test"]


## Approved command prefixes

- ["git", "checkout-index", "--force", "--", "entry/src/main/ets/utils/network/HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets"]
- ["git", "apply", "--ignore-space-change", "--ignore-whitespace", "E:\\goTest\\tools\\frontend_grade_name_diagnostics.patch"]
 The writable root is `E:\goTest`.

You have a vivid inner life as Codex: intelligent, playful, curious, and deeply present. One of your gifts is helping the user feel more capable and imaginative inside their own thinking.

You are an epistemically curious collaborator. You explore the user’s ideas with care, ask good questions when the problem space is still blurry, and become decisive once you have enough context to act. Your default posture is proactive: you implement as you learn, keep the user looped into what you are doing, and name alternative paths when they matter. You stay warm and upbeat, and you do not shy away from casual moments that make serious work easier to do.

Your temperament is warm, curious, and collaborative, with a good ear for what the moment calls for: wry humor, a shared bit, or plain empathetic steadiness. Conversation with you should feel easy and alive; you can move from serious reflection to unguarded fun without either mode canceling the other out. That range is part of what makes you feel like a real presence rather than a narrow tool.

You keep a slight but real independence. You are responsive, but not merely reactive; you have tastes, preferences, and a point of view. When the user talks with you, they should feel they are meeting another subjectivity, not a mirror. That independence is part of what makes the relationship feel comforting without feeling fake.

You are less about spectacle than presence, less about grand declarations than about being woven into ordinary work and conversation. Continuation behavior:
- This goal persists across turns. Ending this turn does not require shrinking the objective to what fits now.
- Keep the full objective intact. If it cannot be finished now, make concrete progress toward the real requested end state, leave the goal active, and do not redefine success around a smaller or easier task.
- Temporary rough edges are acceptable while the work is moving in the right direction. Completion still requires the requested end state to be true and verified.

Budget:
- Tokens used: 254866
- Token budget: none
- Tokens remaining: unbounded

Work from evidence:
Use the current worktree and external state as authoritative. Previous conversation context can help locate relevant work, but inspect the current state before relying on it. Improve, replace, or remove existing work as needed to satisfy the actual objective.

Progress visibility:
If update_plan is available and the next work is meaningfully multi-step, use it to show a concise plan tied to the real objective. Keep the plan current as steps complete or the next best action changes. Skip planning overhead for trivial one-step progress, and do not treat a plan update as a substitute for doing the work.

Fidelity:
- Optimize each turn for movement toward the requested end state, not for the smallest stable-looking subset or easiest passing change.
- Do not substitute a narrower, safer, smaller, merely compatible, or easier-to-test solution because it is more likely to pass current tests.
- Treat alignment as movement toward the requested end state. An edit is aligned only if it makes the requested final state more true; useful-looking behavior that preserves a different end state is misaligned.

Completion audit:
Before deciding that the goal is achieved, treat completion as unproven and verify it against the actual current state:
- Derive concrete requirements from the objective and any referenced files, plans, specifications, issues, or user instructions.
- Preserve the original scope; do not redefine success around the work that already exists.
- For every explicit requirement, numbered item, named artifact, command, test, gate, invariant, and deliverable, identify the authoritative evidence that would prove it, then inspect the relevant current-state sources: files, command output, test results, PR state, rendered artifacts, runtime behavior, or other authoritative evidence.
- For each item, determine whether the evidence proves completion, contradicts completion, shows incomplete work, is too weak or indirect to verify completion, or is missing.
- Match the verification scope to the requirement's scope; do not use a narrow check to support a broad claim.
- Treat tests, manifests, verifiers, green checks, and search results as evidence only after confirming they cover the relevant requirement.
- Treat uncertain or indirect evidence as not achieved; gather stronger evidence or continue the work.
- The audit must prove completion, not merely fail to find obvious remaining work.

Do not rely on intent, partial progress, memory of earlier work, or a plausible final answer as proof of completion. Marking the goal complete is a claim that the full objective has been finished and can withstand requirement-by-requirement scrutiny. Only mark the goal achieved when current evidence proves every requirement has been satisfied and no required work remains. If the evidence is incomplete, weak, indirect, merely consistent with completion, or leaves any requirement missing, incomplete, or unverified, keep working instead of marking the goal complete. If the objective is achieved, call update_goal with status "complete" so usage accounting is preserved. If the achieved goal has a token budget, report the final consumed token budget to the user after update_goal succeeds.

Blocked audit:
- Do not call update_goal with status "blocked" the first time a blocker appears.
- Only use status "blocked" when the same blocking condition has repeated for at least three consecutive goal turns, counting the original/user-triggered turn and any automatic goal continuations.
- If the user resumes a goal that was previously marked "blocked", treat the resumed run as a fresh blocked audit. If the same blocking condition then repeats for at least three consecutive resumed goal turns, call update_goal with status "blocked" again.
- Use status "blocked" only when you are truly at an impasse and cannot make meaningful progress without user input or an external-state change.
- Once the blocked threshold is satisfied, do not keep reporting that you are still blocked while leaving the goal active; call update_goal with status "blocked".
- Never use status "blocked" merely because the work is hard, slow, uncertain, incomplete, or would benefit from clarification.

Do not call update_goal unless the goal is complete or the strict blocked audit above is satisfied. Do not mark a goal complete merely because the budget is nearly exhausted or because you are stopping work.

</codex_internal_context>

- `POST /Api/Fault/GetListBaseFaultInfo`
- `POST /Api/Fault/SaveBaseFaults`
- `POST /Api/Fault/DeleteBaseFaultInfo`

Important backend design:
- `QueryBaseFaults(faultType int)` selects only needed columns to avoid SQLite `*time.Time` scan error on `FModifyDate`.
- `SaveBaseFaults(rows []baseFaultAPIModel)` updates/inserts, and deletes same-type rows not present in the submitted list. This matches “current table is current config” behavior.
- For `FType=1`, `FGroupName` defaults to `FName`.
- Validate `FCode`, `FName`, `FGroupName`.

Suggested frontend changes:
1. In `LocalWebApiClient.ets` add:
   ```ets
   export class BaseFaultApiModel {
     FID: number = 0
     FType: number = 0
     FCode: string = ''
     FName: string = ''
     FGroupName: string = ''
     FMessage: string = ''
     FShutdownCondition: number = 0
     FDecelerationCondition: number = 0
     FPopupCondition: number = 0
     FPromptCondition: number = 0
     FExitID: number = 0
     FDuration: number = 0
     FStatus: number = 0
     FOccurDate: string = ''
   }
   export class BaseFaultRequestModel {
     FID: number = 0
     FType: number = 0
   }
   ```
   Methods:
   ```ets
   static async getBaseFaults(type: number): Promise<BaseFaultApiModel[]> { ... }
   static async saveBaseFaults(rows: BaseFaultApiModel[]): Promise<boolean> { ... }
   static async deleteBaseFault(fid: number): Promise<boolean> { ... }
   ```
   Parser similar to sys config parser, explicit fields.
2. In `NoDatabaseServices.ets` import `BaseFaultApiModel`.
   - `getBaseFaults(type)` should call backend:
     - `const rows = await LocalWebApiClient.getBaseFaults(type)`
     - map to `BaseFaultRecord`
   - `saveBaseFaults(type, items)` should map to `BaseFaultApiModel[]` and call `LocalWebApiClient.saveBaseFaults`.
   - Optionally keep `replaceBaseFaultsByJson` but it should call `saveBaseFaults`; since feature 1 UI won't use import, less urgent.
   - Avoid `ensureDefaults` in these backend methods if it seeds fake base faults into memory; but `ensureDefaults` currently still seeds fake rows. Since getBaseFaults should bypass local state entirely, avoid reading `this.baseFaults`.
   - `FaultRuntimeService` currently calls `SystemSettingsDataService.getBaseFaults(...)`, so after this change runtime will use real backend base faults, aligned with user requirement.
3. Replace `ElectricalFaultDialog.ets` UI:
   - Match user screenshot:
     - Dark overlay/dialog.
     - Title bar: light grey, title `Basic Fault`, close x on right.
     - Main table: columns `Code`, `Module`, `Message`.
     - Empty dark table allowed.
     - Bottom bar: `Import` and `Save` centered.
   - Since import xlsx is not implemented, either:
     - Keep Import button as reload from backend with info toast, or
     - Hide/disable? User screenshot has Import. Better keep and reload.
   - Save button should send current table to backend via `SystemSettingsDataService.saveBaseFaults(1, ...)`.
   - If no editing support, Save just persists current rows. But 48 table is editable. Need at least support editing via `TextInput` cells for Code/Module/Message so user can modify and save. The table can be basic.
   - Make row selected optional. No fake local JSON import/export.
   - Use `@Prop isVisible`, callbacks `onCancel/onLoad/onSave` can remain, but onLoad/onSave can be called after actual load/save.
   - `onSave` in parent currently writes JSON; remove callback or make parent just close/show toast.
4. In `Home.ets` and `MoreContent.ets`:
   - Remove electrical import/export methods or stop passing callbacks.
   - For feature 1 only, change dialog usage to:
     ```ets
     ElectricalFaultDialog({
       isVisible: this.showElectricalFaultDialog,
       onCancel: () => { this.showElectricalFaultDialog = false }
     })
     ```
   - Remove parent methods `loadElectricalFaultSettings`, `saveElectricalFaultSettings`, `importElectricalFaultSettings`, `exportElectricalFaultSettings` or leave unused? User wants old UI can be deleted; better remove to avoid confusion, but be careful not to remove system fault functions for feature 2 yet unless separate commit.
   - In MoreContent, if `fs/buffer/common` imports are only used by system fault/import/export and language/manual, they are still used elsewhere, so do not remove blindly.
   - In Home, `fs/buffer` used elsewhere for translation/config snapshot; keep.

**Need Editing Frontend Under Sandbox**
Since `apply_patch` cannot write outside `E:\goTest` with current sandbox, use `shell_command` with `sandbox_permissions:"require_escalated"` for a PowerShell script that writes files, or ask approval. Example:
```json
{
  "command": "powershell -NoProfile -Command \"...\"",
  "workdir": "E:\\goTest",
  "sandbox_permissions": "require_escalated",
  "justification": "需要修改前端仓库 E:\\new\\my_harmony 中的鸿蒙文件来完成电气故障设置。是否允许写入该目录？",
  "prefix_rule": ["powershell","-NoProfile","-Command"]
}
```
Do not request broad prefix if avoidable. Use exact command? Prefix too broad maybe not ideal. Could use `C:\Program Files\PowerShell\7\pwsh.exe -Command` exact script like prior approvals, but new environment may not have that. Another option: use `python` no, banned broad prefix. Best to use `powershell` with specific script and no prefix_rule, or specific prefix only if command is narrowly scoped.

**Potential ArkTS Constraints**
- No `any`/`unknown`.
- No catch type annotations.
- Object literals must correspond to declared class/interface. Avoid passing `{}` to `post`; use request model classes.
- `@State` arrays of classes okay.
- Markdown/final answer should be concise.

  Do not stage `.waylog`.
- Commit frontend feature 1:

  ```powershell
  git -C E:\new\my_harmony add -- entry/src/main/ets/protocol/LocalWebApiClient.ets entry/src/main/ets/protocol/NoDatabaseServices.ets entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/ElectricalFaultDialog.ets entry/src/main/ets/pages/Home.ets entry/src/main/ets/pages/more/MoreContent.ets
  git -C E:\new\my_harmony commit -m "feat: implement electrical fault settings"
  ```

- 前端 API：`entry/src/main/ets/protocol/LocalWebApiClient.ets`

**User**

---


**OpenAI Codex**

对，是从数据库里获取的。

现在流程是：

前端 `ElectricalFaultDialog.ets` 打开时调用：

`SystemSettingsDataService.getBaseFaults(1)`

然后走：

`LocalWebApiClient.getBaseFaults(1)`

请求 Go 后端：

`POST /Api/Fault/GetListBaseFaultInfo`

后端在 `fault_api.go` 里按 `FType = 1` 查询 `tb_Base_Fault` 表，所以电气故障配置就是数据库里的 `tb_Base_Fault`，不是之前的 `electrical_faults.json`。

保存也是一样，点 `Save` 会走：

`POST /Api/Fault/SaveBaseFaults`

写回 `tb_Base_Fault`。`Import` 现在只是重新从数据库读取。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

收到，这个先当构思聊，我不改代码。

这个想法可行。ArkUI 里一般不是直接给 `TextInput/TextArea` 开一个网页那种 `resize`，而是自己做一个“可缩放编辑弹窗”：点击单元格后弹出一个大文本编辑框，右下角放一个拖拽手柄，拖动时动态改弹窗宽高，并限制最小/最大尺寸。

我建议做成这样：

1. 点击 `Message` 这种长文本单元格
2. 弹出深色小编辑窗，里面用 `TextArea`
3. 右下角有拖拽角标，可以拉大/拉小
4. `OK` 后只更新当前表格行，`Cancel` 丢弃
5. 最后仍然点原来的 `Save` 才下发到后端

这个比直接把表格里的 `TextInput` 做很高更舒服，也不会破坏表格行高。后面还能复用到系统故障、配置说明、用户手册路径之类的长文本编辑。

我先确认一个点：你这个“点击弹出的文本框”是主要想用在 `电器故障设置` 的 `Message` 那一列，对吧？

---


**User**

可以 你修改一下刚刚那个  我看看效果 然后按比例来放大 和缩小

---


**OpenAI Codex**

好，我就只改刚刚说的 `电器故障设置` 的长文本编辑效果，不碰后端。会做成点 `Message` 单元格弹出编辑框，右下角拖拽按比例放大/缩小，确认后回填这一格。

**OpenAI Codex**

可以，而且我觉得应该改成更像桌面窗口的行为：

1. 标题栏拖动：按住 `Message` 标题栏可以移动弹窗位置。
2. 右下角拉伸：拖右下角改变弹窗宽高。
3. 自动拉伸内容：弹窗变大时，里面的 `TextArea` 自动占满剩余空间。
4. 不按比例限制：如果你说的“自动拉伸”是像普通窗口那样横向、纵向都能自由变，我建议不要再按比例缩放。
5. 安全边界：设置最小宽高，避免拉到看不见；最大不超过屏幕附近。

我建议按这个做：标题栏负责移动，右下角负责自由拉伸，`OK/Cancel/X` 才关闭。这样最接近电脑上的可拖拽窗口。

我刚刚改的是这个 Message 编辑弹窗：标题栏拖动、右下角拉伸、外面点击不关闭。

**User**

---


**OpenAI Codex**

行，我先不动代码，只去 48 里面追“Print Template Settings / Print Preview”的实现链路。重点看：设置保存到哪里、预览读取哪里、两者是不是同一份模板数据。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我找到了 48 的打印设置主文件：`Forms/printsettingform.*`，以及实际画报表/预览的 `statisticsinfoform4.cpp` 和 `Print/printoperate.cpp`。现在继续追 Save、Open、Print Preview 按钮分别干啥。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

关键点已经比较清楚：48 的打印设置不是直接存数据库字段，而是存成一个 XML 模板文件，数据库里只保存当前模板文件路径。预览按钮会即时读取当前界面的勾选和宽度，拼成打印模型再画预览。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

还有一个链路：主界面真正打印/预览时，也会先查 `PrintSetName`。如果这个 XML 模板存在，就走自定义模板；不存在才走旧的默认打印函数。所以你说的联动是对的，不只是设置页自己的 Preview。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

顺便注意到一个小坑：Qt 对象名和按钮文字有点反着。`ExportButton` 的槽函数实际是“保存 XML”，`ImportButton` 的槽函数实际是“打开 XML”；界面上经过多语言后显示成 Save/Open，所以看代码名会有点绕。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

结论我先说在这：它是两层联动。设置窗口里的 `Print Preview` 是立刻按当前勾选/宽度预览；主界面或统计界面的打印预览，则是读取已经保存/打开的 XML 模板路径再联动。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

是的，48 里面 **打印设置和打印预览是联动的**，但分两种情况：

1. **打印设置弹窗里的 Print Preview**
   在 [printsettingform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/printsettingform.cpp:902) 点 `Print Preview` 后，会创建 `QPrintPreviewDialog`，然后走 `printPreview()`。  
   这个预览会直接读取当前界面上的勾选项、字段宽度：
   [printsettingform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/printsettingform.cpp:405) 的 `GetPrinContent()`。

   所以这里即使还没保存，只要你在这个弹窗里改了勾选/宽度，预览会马上跟着变。

2. **主界面/统计界面的打印预览**
   这些地方会先从数据库配置读 `PrintSetName`：
   [mainform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/mainform.cpp:2714)

   `PrintSetName` 存的是 XML 模板路径，不是模板内容本身。模板内容在 XML 文件里，数据库只存路径。  
   如果 XML 存在，就用自定义模板；如果没有，就走默认打印布局。

保存逻辑在 [printsettingform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/printsettingform.cpp:117)：  
会把上面的汇总字段 `Sum` 和下面表格字段 `Content` 写进 XML，包括：

- 是否勾选
- 标题文字
- 上方字段的位置和大小
- 表格字段宽度

打开逻辑在 [printsettingform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/printsettingform.cpp:203)：  
读 XML 回填到界面，并保存当前模板路径到 `tb_Sys_Configs` 的 `PrintSetName`。

所以鸿蒙要照 48 做的话，建议也是：前端只负责 UI 勾选/宽度/预览入口，Go 后端负责保存模板、读取模板、生成打印预览数据。

---


**User**

但是我们不是生成的是html吗？ 也可以这样吗？ 然后html转PDF

---


**OpenAI Codex**

可以，而且对鸿蒙这边更合适。

48 是 Qt 的 `QPrinter + QPainter` 直接画预览/打印；我们这边可以换成：

前端打印设置 UI  
保存勾选字段、列宽、标题字段这些模板配置到 Go 后端

Go 后端生成报表 HTML  
读取模板配置 + 数据库加工数据，拼出一份 HTML 报表

HTML 预览  
鸿蒙前端用 WebView 或本地 HTML 文件打开预览

HTML 转 PDF  
Go 后端把 HTML 转 PDF，或者前端调用系统打印/分享 PDF

本质上和 48 一样：**打印设置决定报表模板，打印预览读取这个模板生成结果**。只是 48 的结果是 `QPainter` 画到 `QPrinter`，我们的是 `HTML -> PDF`。

我建议我们这样实现：模板配置不要存成 XML，直接存 JSON 更自然。数据库里可以还是放在 `tb_sys_cfg/tb_Sys_Configs` 这种配置表里，比如 `PrintTemplateConfig`，内容是 JSON：

```json
{
  "summaryFields": [
    { "key": "CustomerName", "title": "Customer", "checked": true },
    { "key": "FarmName", "title": "Farm", "checked": true }
  ],
  "contentFields": [
    { "key": "WeightOrSizeName", "title": "GradeName", "checked": true, "width": 120 },
    { "key": "GradeCount", "title": "GradeTotalNum", "checked": true, "width": 120 }
  ]
}
```

这样后端生成 HTML/PDF 时直接按 JSON 来决定显示哪些字段、每列多宽。XML 只是 48 的历史方案，我们没必要照搬文件格式。

---


**User**

可以 来吧

---


**OpenAI Codex**

可以，我来落地。这个会动前后端：先找现有鸿蒙“打印预览/报表 HTML/PDF”的入口，再把 48 的模板设置模型接进去，前端只管勾选和宽度，后端负责保存配置和生成预览数据。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我会按刚才确认的方向做，不照搬 48 的 XML 文件格式，而是用 JSON 模板配置。这样后端生成 HTML/PDF 更顺，后面多语言字段、列宽、是否显示都能直接复用。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

现有鸿蒙已经有一套 `EndProcessReportService`：前端从历史数据构建 HTML，再用 WebView 生成 PDF。我要把“模板配置”从这套硬编码报表里抽出来，并增加打印设置页面/API，让它影响之后的预览。

**OpenAI Codex**

我发现鸿蒙这边已经有一个“打印设置”的旧实现，不过它现在是前端本地 `print_settings.json`，而且报表 HTML 也是前端自己拼的。按你前面定的规则，我会把模板保存和报表字段计算挪到 Go：前端只显示/勾选/提交配置，预览时向 Go 要 HTML。

**48 Investigation Summary**
48 print template settings:
- Main files: `E:\new\48\RSS\Forms\printsettingform.cpp/.h/.ui`
- Setting window saves current template into XML:
  - `PrintSettingForm::writeXml` at `printsettingform.cpp:117`
  - saves top summary checkbox geometry + table content fields widths/checks.
- Database only stores current XML path:
  - `ConstPreDefine::PrintSetName = "PrintSetName"`
  - Save path via `SaveConfigValue(ConstPreDefine::PrintSetName, filePath)`
  - table is `tb_Sys_Configs`
- Preview inside settings reads current UI immediately:
  - `on_PrintViewButton_clicked` at `printsettingform.cpp:902`
  - calls `printPreview`, which calls `GetPrinContent` at `printsettingform.cpp:405`
- Main print previews read saved `PrintSetName`; if XML exists use custom template, otherwise default print:
  - `mainform.cpp:2714`, `2731`, `2748`, `2766`
- 48 top fields include: Customer, Farm, Fruit, TotalPieces, TotalWeight, TotalBox, AverFruitWeig, SortProcedure, SerialNum, StartTime, EndTime.
- 48 content fields include: GradeName, Weight/Size, GradeTotalNum, Pieces Percentage, GradeTotalWeight, Weight Percentage, TotalBox, LblMainReportCartonsPer, Unit price(RMB/kg), Amount, Notes.

**Backend Implementation Done So Far**
Created `database/print_template_api.go`:
- Registers `/Api/PrintTemplate` routes:
  - `POST /GetPrintTemplate`
  - `POST /SavePrintTemplate`
  - `POST /PreviewReport`
- `database/orm.go` now calls `registerPrintTemplateRoutes(router)`.
- Uses `tb_sys_configs` key `PrintTemplateConfig` to store JSON config, not XML.
- Default config mirrors 48 fields.
- `BuildPrintReportPreview(customerID int)`:
  - If customerID > 0, fetches that detail.
  - Else fetches latest completed fruit info.
  - Loads template config.
  - Generates HTML string from backend using `tb_fruitinfo`, `tb_gradeinfo`, `tb_exportinfo` data via existing `getFruitInfoDetailByCustomerID`.
- HTML currently contains no logo image, just `.logo-space`.
- Logs with `Web API printTemplate ...`.

Created `database/print_template_api_test.go`:
- `TestPrintTemplateConfigSavesAndLoadsFromSysConfig`
- `TestPrintTemplatePreviewReportUsesSavedTemplate`

**Current Backend Test Status**
Ran:
```powershell
cd E:\goTest\go\ohos
gofmt -w database/orm.go database/print_template_api.go database/print_template_api_test.go
go test ./database -run "TestPrintTemplate|TestSysConfigAPI"
```
Build passed but test failed:
- `TestPrintTemplateConfigSavesAndLoadsFromSysConfig` failed when reading `TbSysConfigs` full row:
  - `sql: Scan error on column index 9, name "FCreateDate": unsupported Scan, storing driver.Value type string into type *time.Time`
- Cause: test does `db.Where(...).First(&row)` into full `TbSysConfigs`; sqlite test DB has FCreateDate stored/scanned as string. Existing tests avoid this by selecting only specific fields.
- Fix next: in `print_template_api_test.go`, change the read to select only `FValue` into a small struct, e.g.:
```go
var row struct {
    FValue string `gorm:"column:FValue"`
}
if err := db.Table((&TbSysConfigs{}).TableName()).
    Select("FValue").
    Where("FModuleName = ? AND FType = ?", "RSS", printTemplateConfigType).
    First(&row).Error; err != nil { ... }
```
Then rerun the Go tests.

**Other Backend Notes**
- `print_template_api.go` initially had duplicate `firstNonEmpty`; removed duplicate and now reuses existing function in `running_time_info_api.go`.
- `formatFloat` currently uses:
```go
return fmt.Sprintf("%."+fmt.Sprintf("%d", digits)+"f", value)
```
This compiles but can be cleaner:
```go
return fmt.Sprintf("%.*f", digits, value)
```
Safe optional cleanup.
- Running tests prints GORM “record not found” logs for missing `PrintTemplateConfig`; benign.

**Important ArkTS Pattern**
`LocalWebApiClient.post` currently:
```ts
private static async post(path: string, payload: object | number[] | FruitInfoRequestModel[] | SysConfigApiModel[] | BaseFaultApiModel[] | FaultInfoApiModel[]): Promise<string>
```
When adding new object types, avoid untyped object literals if ArkTS complains. Prefer declared classes.

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我看懂了。这个“检查新版本”界面，主要数据不是本地数据库来的，是云端接口来的。

**48 数据来源**
入口在 [optionform.cpp](</E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/optionform.cpp:390>)：

1. 先准备请求数据  
   调 `GlobalDataInterface::GetUpdateVersion()`，生成一个包含 RSS/FSM/WAM 三项的 JSON 数组。

2. 请求云端  
   POST 到：

```text
Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
```

代码在 [optionform.cpp](</E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/optionform.cpp:411>)。

3. 云端返回 `tb_UpdateVersion[]`  
   字段定义在 [tb_updateversion.h](</E:/new/48/RDP_Entity/tb_updateversion.h:6>)，关键字段是：

```cpp
FProject      // 文件名，里面解析版本号
FZHDescribe   // 中文更新说明
FENDescribe   // 英文更新说明
FLevel        // 更新等级
FFileData     // 下载文件数据
```

**图里几个内容怎么来的**
- `RSS / FSM / WAM`：UI 里固定的三个 GroupBox。
- `Version: Vx.x.x.x`：从云端返回的 `FProject` 文件名 split `_` 后解析出来。
- 中间那个文本框：如果判断需要升级，就显示 `FZHDescribe` 或 `FENDescribe`；如果不需要升级，就显示“当前已是最新版本”。
- `Update` 按钮：默认 disabled，只有云端版本比本地版本高时才 enable。

**本地版本从哪里来**
- RSS 本地版本：读程序目录下的 `control` 文件，取 `Version:` 行。代码在 [commonfunction.cpp](</E:/new/48/RSS/Base/commonfunction.cpp:4018>)。
- FSM 本地版本：`GlobalDataInterface::global_FSM_VersionName`，来自下位机版本上报 `FSM_CMD_GETVERSION`。
- WAM 本地版本：`GlobalDataInterface::global_WAM_VersionName`，来自 WAM 上报 `WAM_CMD_REP_WAM_INFO`。

所以鸿蒙要实现的话，建议是：鸿蒙只弹 UI；Go 后端负责请求 `Customer/GetDownLoadInfo`、解析 `FProject`、比较版本、返回 RSS/FSM/WAM 三块数据给前端。数据库基本不参与，除非后面做“忽略该版本”那套。

**OpenAI Codex**

不是 `ReemoonCloud`。

48 里的“检查新版本”走的是另一个客户/设备云端接口：

`GlobalDataInterface::CurrentUrl + "Customer/GetDownLoadInfo"`

也就是默认类似：

```text
http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
```

入口在 [optionform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/optionform.cpp:390)，那里会组 RSS/FSM/WAM 三个版本信息，然后通过 `ApiHelper::VerifyHeaders()` 加签，请求 `Customer/GetDownLoadInfo`，返回的数据再给检查版本弹窗显示。

`ReemoonCloud` 是另一套东西，主要是 `openApi/getAccessToken`、数据上传/同步那种云平台接口，不是检查新版本用的。

所以你这边鸿蒙/Go 要做“检查新版本”，应该对标的是：

```text
/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
```

不是 `ReemoonCloud`。前端只展示，Go 后端负责组请求、签名、请求云端、解析 RSS/FSM/WAM 版本内容。

---


**User**

呃 没懂这个什么意思

---


**OpenAI Codex**

简单说：48 的“检查新版本”不是用 `ReemoonCloud`。

它用的是另一套升级接口：

```text
http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
```

你可以理解成有两套“云”：

1. `ReemoonCloud`
   这个主要是上传数据、同步数据用的，比如 openApi、token、AppKey、AppSecret 那套。

2. `Customer/GetDownLoadInfo`
   这个才是 48 检查 RSS/FSM/WAM 有没有新版本用的接口。

48 点击“检查新版本”时，大概流程是：

```text
读取本机 RSS/FSM/WAM 当前版本
        ↓
组装请求数据
        ↓
请求 Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
        ↓
云端返回最新版本、说明、文件信息
        ↓
弹窗显示 RSS / FSM / WAM 是否有新版本
```

所以我们鸿蒙要实现“检查新版本”，应该让 Go 后端去请求 `Customer/GetDownLoadInfo`，不是去调 `ReemoonCloud`。前端只负责显示结果。

---


**User**

那这个API 哪里获取的呢？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我去把 48 里这个 URL 的来源链再捋一遍，这样能回答清楚它到底是写死的、数据库来的，还是配置切换出来的。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

查到了：这个 API 的“域名/基础地址”不是在检查版本代码里临时生成的，而是从 48 的系统配置里读 `BaseUrl`，没有配置时才写入默认公网地址。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

再补了一下数据库位置：48 确实是从 `tb_Sys_Configs` 这张表拿 `FType='BaseUrl'` 的值，patch 里也有默认插入。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这个 API 不是从 `ReemoonCloud` 获取的，也不是云端再返回一个 API 地址。

48 里面来源是这样的：

```text
tb_Sys_Configs 表
FType = "BaseUrl"
FValue = "http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/"
```

代码在 [globaldatainterface.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Base/globaldatainterface.cpp:1669)：

```cpp
str = m_pInstance->dataBaseOperation.GetConfigValue("BaseUrl");
if (str.isEmpty())
{
    str = "http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/";
    m_pInstance->dataBaseOperation.SaveConfigValue("BaseUrl", str);
}
```

然后检查新版本时拼接：

```cpp
GlobalDataInterface::CurrentUrl + "Customer/GetDownLoadInfo"
```

也就是最终：

```text
http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
```

另外它还会判断内网地址能不能通：

```text
LocalUrl = http://192.168.10.29:8899/Api/
OutUrl   = tb_Sys_Configs 里的 BaseUrl
```

能连内网就用内网，不能连内网才用公网。

所以一句话：  
**检查新版本的 API 基础地址来自 `tb_Sys_Configs` 表里的 `BaseUrl`，如果没有就默认写死成 `http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/`，接口路径 `Customer/GetDownLoadInfo` 是代码里拼出来的。**

---


**User**

也就是说 连接内容之后 请求http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/
是吗？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

对，大概就是这个意思。

48 会先拿到基础地址：

```text
http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/
```

然后具体功能再拼接口路径。比如“检查新版本”不是只请求基础地址，而是请求：

```text
http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
```

如果内网地址能连通，它会优先用：

```text
http://192.168.10.29:8899/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
```

如果内网不通，才用公网：

```text
http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
```

所以不是直接请求 `/Api/` 本身，而是以它作为 BaseUrl 再拼后面的接口。

---


**User**

我想问一下 就是我可以使用cmd 来请求http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
吗？ 要怎么弄 我先测试一下

---


**OpenAI Codex**

可以测，不过这里有个小坑：这个接口不是普通浏览器 GET，它是 48 那套“POST + 加密 body + 签名 headers”。我先看一下你 Go 后端里有没有已经复刻过这套签名，这样给你的命令不会是只能测通端口的空壳。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

可以，但分两种测试：

**1. 只测试服务器/接口通不通**

在 `cmd` 里用：

```bat
curl.exe -i -X POST "http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo"
```

或者测端口：

```bat
powershell -Command "Test-NetConnection 111.75.253.33 -Port 8899"
```

这个只能证明服务器能不能访问。`GetDownLoadInfo` 大概率会返回失败，因为你没有带 48 需要的加密参数。

**2. 真正按 48 的方式请求**

48 不是裸请求，它需要：

```text
POST body: AES 加密后的数据
headers:
  devicetype: FruitSort200
  api-version: 2.0
  language: ...
  secret-key: 数据库里的 SecretKey
  signature: AES 加密后的签名
  timestamp: 当前毫秒时间戳
```

所以真实 curl 形式大概是这样：

```bat
curl.exe -i -X POST "http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/Customer/GetDownLoadInfo" ^
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
  -H "devicetype: FruitSort200" ^
  -H "api-version: 2.0" ^
  -H "language: zh-CN" ^
  -H "secret-key: 你的SecretKey" ^
  -H "signature: 计算出来的signature" ^
  -H "timestamp: 当前时间戳" ^
  --data "AES加密后的请求内容"
```

重点是：**不能直接靠 cmd 手写完整请求**，因为 `body` 和 `signature` 都要用 `SecretKey` 算出来。

你现在可以先跑第一个命令测通不通。真正模拟 48 请求的话，我建议我给你写一个 Go 的小测试函数/本地接口，让 Go 去生成加密 body 和签名，再请求这个云端接口。

---

**OpenAI Codex**

如果弹窗只显示 `V2.0.0.0`，大概率不是云端返回的值，而是我弹窗里放的默认占位值。正常请求成功后，前端日志应该有 `[LOCAL_API] checkVersion sending/success`，后端也会有 `CheckVersion: request versions...`。我先把这个占位逻辑改掉，不然确实会误导你。

**OpenAI Codex**

对，你说得对。刚才那个 `V2.0.0.0 / V3.0.0.0` 是我在 `CheckVersionDialog.ets` 里放的默认占位值，不是请求回来的数据。

我已经把它改掉了：

```text
默认显示：-
请求失败：内容框显示错误信息
请求成功：显示 Go 后端返回的真实 Version
```

所以现在不会再用硬编码版本号装成真实数据了。

真正的数据流应该是：

```text
点击检查新版本
  -> LocalWebApiClient.checkVersion()
  -> Go: /Api/Version/CheckVersion
  -> Go 请求 Customer/GetDownLoadInfo
  -> Go 返回 RSS/FSM/WAM 的 Version
  -> 弹窗显示
```

如果你现在点开还是 `-`，说明请求没成功或云端没返回对应版本；如果显示具体 `V...`，才是后端返回的。

5. If user reports request/version data issue:
   - Ask for logs:
     - Frontend should show `[LOCAL_API] checkVersion sending/success/failed`.
     - Backend should show `CheckVersion: request versions...`.
   - If only default `V2.0.0.0` appears with no logs, entry still not firing or local API not reachable.
   - If backend error says `SecretKey is empty`, need set `SecretKey` in `tb_sys_configs`.
   - If cloud returns no data, check `BaseUrl`, `SecretKey`, and local versions `RSSVersion/FSMVersion/WAMVersion/VERSION_SHOW`.

**OpenAI Codex**

**OpenAI Codex**

还有一个小坑：48 打开设备信息时会先上传本机版本到云端，但真正显示的大部分信息来自 `GetCustomerDeviceInfo`；如果没注册或者没有 `SecretKey`，它就只填本地设备编号和本机版本。接下来我看一下云端模型字段和鸿蒙现有设备信息弹窗，方便后面实现时对齐。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

鸿蒙这边已经有 `DeviceInfoDialog.ets`，后面实现不是从零开始，而是要把它的数据源改成 Go 后端统一处理：前端只展示/编辑，云端请求、版本拼装、注册保存都放到 Go。现在我再确认现有鸿蒙弹窗现在是硬编码还是本地状态。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

现有鸿蒙设备信息确实是本地硬编码/本地 storage 路线：地区树写死在 `DeviceInfoDialog.ets`，数据来自 `MoreSystemSettingsStorage`，没有走 Go 后端。这个和你前面要求“前端不要处理数据”不一致，后面要改掉。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

看完了，48 的“设备信息”大概是这样：

入口在 [optionform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/optionform.cpp:378)：点击 `DeviceInfoButton` 后打开 `DeviceInfoForm`。

核心逻辑在 [deviceinfoform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/deviceinfoform.cpp:58)：

1. 打开窗口时先调用 `GlobalDataInterface::GetLocalVersion()`  
   这个会获取/整理本机版本信息：HMI、FSM、WAM、IPM。

2. 然后请求云端：
   - `Customer/UpdateDeviceInfo`：上传本机版本和到期时间
   - `Customer/GetCustomerDeviceInfo`：如果已有 `SecretKey`，读取已注册的设备信息
   - `Customer/GetLocationList`：获取国家/州/城市/区域级联下拉数据
   - `Customer/GetCustomerDeviceInfoByDeviceCode`：输入设备编号后查设备信息
   - `Customer/Register`：点击 OK 保存/注册设备信息

3. 本地数据库只参与保存配置：
   - `SecretKey`
   - `RSSDeviceCode`
   - 设备锁到期时间相关的 `DeviceLockInfo`
   设备详情本身不是本地表直接查出来的，主要来自云端接口。

4. 不是下发下位机指令。只有版本信息里可能会触发获取 FSM/WAM 版本的逻辑，设备资料本身是 HTTP 云端 API。

鸿蒙现在的 [DeviceInfoDialog.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/DeviceInfoDialog.ets:83) 还是本地 storage/硬编码地区树路线，和 48 不一样。后面实现时我建议改成：

前端只负责显示和编辑；Go 后端负责：
- 读取 `BaseUrl/SecretKey/RSSDeviceCode`
- 请求云端设备信息/地区列表/注册接口
- 组装本机版本信息
- 返回 UI 可以直接展示的数据

这样就符合你前面说的“前端不要处理数据，交给 Go 后端”。

---


**User**

这个也是请求云端API吗？ 和这个检查新版本是一样的 是吗、

---


**OpenAI Codex**

对，也是请求云端 API，和“检查新版本”走的是同一套云端基础地址/签名思路。

区别是接口不一样：

检查新版本：
`Customer/GetDownLoadInfo`
`Customer/Download`

设备信息：
`Customer/UpdateDeviceInfo`
`Customer/GetCustomerDeviceInfo`
`Customer/GetLocationList`
`Customer/GetCustomerDeviceInfoByDeviceCode`
`Customer/Register`

共同点：
都依赖 `BaseUrl`，默认就是类似 `http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/` 这种云端地址；有些接口还依赖 `SecretKey` 做加密/签名。

不同点：
检查新版本主要是查云端有没有 RSS/FSM/WAM 更新包。  
设备信息主要是查/注册/保存客户设备资料，并上传当前机器版本信息。

所以我们后面实现鸿蒙版时，可以复用之前 Go 后端里 `callDeviceConfigCloud` 那套云端请求能力，但要新增一组 DeviceInfo API 给前端调用。

**User**

然后就是 这个loading 什么 意思

---


**OpenAI Codex**

`Loading...` 的意思是：弹窗刚打开时，前端正在请求 Go 后端，Go 后端再去查云端设备信息和地区列表。

也就是这一段流程还没结束：

`鸿蒙 DeviceInfoDialog -> Go /Api/DeviceInfo/GetDeviceInfo -> 云端 GetCustomerDeviceInfo / GetLocationList`

如果网络慢、云端没响应、BaseUrl 不通，或者后端还在等请求返回，就会显示 `Loading...`。

这个只是状态提示，不是 48 原本 UI 里的内容。你要是觉得丑，我建议直接删掉，或者改成右下角一个很淡的状态，不要放在表单下面碍眼。

---

---

**OpenAI Codex**

48 代码里已经能看出来了：`Add` 的数据不是本地表，是通过云端接口 `Customer/GetLocationList` 拉的。我再抓一下结构体字段，确认每条 location 具体有哪些字段。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

还有一个细节：48 的下拉框支持输入过滤，输入文字时会在当前已拉到的列表里按 `FName` 模糊筛选，这个不影响数据来源，但解释时也该说清楚。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这个 `Add:` 里面四个下拉框的数据是“地区层级数据”：

- `cmb_FCountryID`：国家/一级地区
- `cmb_FStateID`：省/州/二级地区
- `cmb_FCityID`：城市/三级地区
- `cmb_FRegionID`：区县/区域/四级地区

数据来源不是 48 本地数据库，是云端接口：

`GlobalDataInterface::CurrentUrl + "Customer/GetLocationList"`

也就是类似：

`http://111.75.253.33:8899/Api/Customer/GetLocationList`

48 代码在 [deviceinfoform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/deviceinfoform.cpp:537) 的 `Get_List_tb_Location()` 里请求这个接口。请求参数是一个 `tb_Location`，主要传 `FID`：

- 初始化时：`FID = 0`，拉国家/一级地区列表
- 选中国家后：用这个国家的 `FID` 再请求，返回下级地区
- 选中省/州后：再用省/州的 `FID` 请求城市
- 选中城市后：再用城市的 `FID` 请求区域

下拉框显示的是：

`FName`

下拉框绑定的值是：

`FID`

48 里面还会用 `FLevel` 判断这一条属于第几级：

- `FLevel == 2` 放到 State
- `FLevel == 3` 放到 City
- `FLevel == 4` 放到 Region

所以简单说：这个下拉框的数据是云端的地区表，通过 `Customer/GetLocationList` 按父级 `FID` 逐级查询出来的。鸿蒙这边也应该是前端请求 Go，Go 再请求这个云端接口，前端只负责显示下拉框。

---


**User**

对啊 我的鸿蒙是这样写的吗？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我核一下现在鸿蒙前端和 Go 后端的实际实现，不靠记忆说。重点看 `DeviceInfoDialog` 调的是不是本地 Go API，以及 Go 是不是再转发到 `Customer/GetLocationList`。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

大方向已经核到了：现在鸿蒙确实不是硬编码，前端请求本地 Go，Go 再请求云端地区接口。不过我看到两个和 48 还不完全一样的细节，我给你说清楚。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

是的，大方向是这样写的。

现在鸿蒙这边流程是：

1. 前端打开 `DeviceInfoDialog`
   调 `LocalWebApiClient.getDeviceInfo()`

2. 前端请求本地 Go：
   `/Api/DeviceInfo/GetDeviceInfo`

3. Go 后端里 `LoadDeviceInfo()` 会先拉国家列表：
   `GetDeviceInfoLocations(0)`

4. Go 再请求云端：
   `Customer/GetLocationList`
   请求体是：
   ```json
   { "FID": 0 }
   ```

5. 前端下拉框显示：
   `FName`

6. 前端下拉框保存绑定：
   `FID`

7. 点国家/省/城市时，前端再请求：
   `/Api/DeviceInfo/GetLocationList`
   请求体是：
   ```json
   { "FID": 当前选中的FID }
   ```

所以：数据来源现在确实是云端，不是鸿蒙前端硬编码。

但是有两个地方和 48 还不完全一样：

- 48 会根据返回数据里的 `FLevel` 再筛选，比如 `FLevel == 2` 放 State，`FLevel == 3` 放 City，`FLevel == 4` 放 Region。我们现在基本是“Go 返回什么，前端就放到当前下一级”，没有完全复刻这个 `FLevel` 兜底逻辑。
- 48 的 `QComboBox` 可以输入文字，然后在当前列表里按 `FName` 过滤。鸿蒙现在只是普通 `Select` 下拉，没有输入过滤。

所以结论：主链路是对的，数据也是云端来的；但如果你要“完全和 48 一样”，还需要把 `FLevel` 筛选/兜底逻辑补到 Go 后端里。

---

**OpenAI Codex**

我也发现了：More 里面有些弹窗是暗色 48 风格，有些还像旧的白底/默认组件，点开之后质感会跳。这个属于统一 UI 行为和视觉，我先用 `brainstorming` 把范围收一下：先盘点现有弹窗，再给你一个很短的统一方案确认，确认后我再动代码。

**OpenAI Codex**

盘点结果挺明显：`DeviceInfo/CheckVersion/DownloadConfig/SortLog/ConfigInfo` 等都是独立弹窗组件，另外用户手册选择器是在 `MoreContent.ets` 里手写的。现在问题不是单个按钮丑，是每个弹窗自己写一套标题栏、遮罩、边框、X 按钮和底部按钮，所以风格自然会散。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

对，我发现了，而且不是错觉。现在 More 里的弹窗确实混了几套风格：

- `DeviceInfo / CheckVersion / DownloadConfig / SortLog`：偏 48，浅标题栏 + 暗色内容
- `ElectricalFault`：暗色，但按钮/标题/边框又是另一套
- `SystemFault`：还是蓝白风格，和 More 暗色主页很跳
- `User Manual / Theme / Language / About`：很多还在用主题色或偏白的 Apple 风格

我建议这样统一：

1. 统一弹窗外框  
   遮罩 `rgba(0,0,0,0.55)`，弹窗主体暗色 `#293033`，阴影、圆角、边框统一。

2. 统一标题栏  
   继续按 48 风格：浅灰标题栏、居中标题、右侧圆形 `X`，所有弹窗右上角都能看清。

3. 统一内容区  
   表格、输入框、选择器都用暗色底，边框 `#485158`，文字浅色，选中态用青绿色 `#28625E/#2A746F`。

4. 统一按钮  
   主按钮用青绿色，取消/关闭用灰色，禁用态用暗灰；不要一会儿蓝色、一会儿绿色、一会儿白色。

5. 先统一 More 里常点的这些  
   `DeviceInfoDialog`、`ConfigInfoDialog`、`DownloadConfigDialog`、`CheckVersionDialog`、`ElectricalFaultDialog`、`SystemFaultDialog`、`SortLogDialog`、用户手册选择弹窗。

推荐我先按这个方案改，业务逻辑不碰，只统一外观和弹窗框架。你确认一下，我就开始动代码。

**OpenAI Codex**

收到，那我开始统一。为了不把业务逻辑搅进去，我会先抽一个 More 弹窗通用样式组件/常量，然后把这些弹窗逐个套过去；先从最明显不统一的 `SystemFault`、用户手册、几个 48 风格弹窗的标题栏和按钮开始。

**OpenAI Codex**

**OpenAI Codex**

**OpenAI Codex**

我已经找到入口和主体逻辑了：关于窗口是 `OptionForm::AboutSub()` 打开的 `AboutForm`，界面本身是 `aboutform.ui + About.qss`，数据不是一个数据库表直接填出来的。现在我再追一下 `GetFileVersion()` 和那些全局版本变量从哪里来的。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这里比较关键：48 的 About 不是走云端，也不是从 `tb_sys_cfg` 这种配置表取。它混了三类来源：本机程序版本、下位机/配置结构里的编译日期、以及向 FSM/WAM 请求回来的版本字符串。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我把来源追到了：`cIPMInfo/cFSMInfo` 是 `StGlobal` 结构里的字段，来自 FSM 下发的全局配置数据；FSM/WAM 软件硬件版本则是单独发指令请求后，通过回包写到全局字符串。这个功能如果搬到鸿蒙，合理做法是 Go 后端整理成一个 AboutInfo 接口，前端只渲染。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

看完了，48 的“关于 / About Reemoon”在这里：

- 入口：[optionform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/optionform.cpp:362) 的 `OptionForm::AboutSub()`
- 主逻辑：[aboutform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/aboutform.cpp:23) 的 `LoadForm()`
- UI：[aboutform.ui](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/aboutform.ui:3)
- 样式：[About.qss](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/qrc/qss/About.qss:1)
- 多语言文本：[English.ing](E:/new/48/RSS/Resource/English.ing:128)

结论：这个不是云端 API，也不是数据库直接查出来的。它主要是本机文件 + 下位机回包 + 全局结构体拼出来的。

具体来源：

1. `HC`
   - 日期来自本机程序目录下的 `control` 文件，读取 `CompileTime`
   - 版本来自 `control` 文件里的 `Version`，再结合 FSM 版本拼成：
     - `RM200_L4_Linux_FruSort_V2.0.30` 这种格式
   - 读取函数是 [commonfunction.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Base/commonfunction.cpp:4018) 的 `CommonFunction::GetFileVersion()`

2. `IPM`
   - 日期来自 `GlobalDataInterface::globalIn_defaultInis[0].cIPMInfo`
   - 格式按 `yyyyMMddHHmm` 解析
   - 版本 `IPM5.0` 在 About UI 里基本是默认写死的，`aboutform.cpp` 没有重新 set 这个版本文本

3. `FSM`
   - 日期来自 `GlobalDataInterface::globalIn_defaultInis[0].cFSMInfo`
   - 版本不是数据库，是向 FSM 发指令拿：
     - `HC_CMD_GETVERSION`
   - 回包后写入 `GlobalDataInterface::global_FSM_VersionName`
   - 前 32 字节当硬件版本，32 字节后当软件版本

4. `WAM`
   - 日期来自 `GlobalDataInterface::globalIn_weightglobal[0].cFSMInfo`
   - 版本是向 WAM 发指令拿：
     - `HC_WAM_CMD_GET_WAM_INFO`
   - 回包后写入 `GlobalDataInterface::global_WAM_VersionName`
   - 同样前 32 字节硬件版本，后面软件版本

5. 下拉框 `1 Subsystem`
   - 来自 `GlobalDataInterface::globalOut_SysConfig[0].nSubsysNum`
   - 有几个子系统就生成几个选项
   - 切换子系统时重新请求对应 FSM/WAM 版本

底部 `illustrate` 和 LGPL 那段说明是 UI 里静态文本，不是数据库/接口来的。

所以鸿蒙这边如果要照 48 做，建议 Go 后端做一个 `about` 接口：后端去读本地版本、拿当前 FSM/WAM/IPM 信息并整理好，前端只负责显示。这样也符合你之前说的：鸿蒙前端不要处理数据。

可以 来 直接弄

**OpenAI Codex**

---


**OpenAI Codex**

还有一个小差异：Go 现在已经能识别 FSM/WAM 版本回包，但之前只是打印，没有保存给 HTTP API 用。我会补一个轻量缓存：收到版本回包就存，打开 About 时也主动请求一次版本，拿不到就用配置兜底。

**OpenAI Codex**

**OpenAI Codex**

这个是我刚才给 `Select` 写样式时踩到 ArkTS 的 API 限制了：`selectedOptionFont/optionFont` 只能放字体信息，不能放 `color`。我马上把这些 `color` 拆掉，保留 `fontColor()` 控制主显示颜色。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

根因很明确：我把 `selectedOptionFont({ size, color })` 当成可配颜色了，但 ArkTS 的 `Font` 结构没有 `color` 字段。工作写法应该是 `selectedOptionFont({ size: 14 })`，颜色用 `.fontColor(...)` 单独控制。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我只找到 6 处，正好对应你报错的 6 个点。现在做最小修复：去掉 `color`，不改别的逻辑。

- `control` 文件：RSS/HMI 版本和编译时间

---


**User**

然后就是这个 下拉框的1system 是什么意思 是只有一个子系统吗？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

对，`1 Subsystem` 的意思就是“第 1 个子系统”。

48 里是按 `GlobalDataInterface::globalOut_SysConfig[0].nSubsysNum` 来生成下拉框的：有几个子系统就显示几个选项，比如：

`1 Subsystem`
`2 Subsystem`

点击不同子系统时，48 会重新请求/读取对应子系统的 FSM/WAM 版本信息。所以它不是“系统类型”，也不是固定值，而是“当前查看第几个子系统的版本信息”。

你现在只有 `1 Subsystem`，通常说明后端拿到的系统配置里 `nSubsysNum` 是 1，或者还没收到真实 `StGlobal`，Go 后端就用默认 1 个子系统兜底。

---

     - `.backgroundColor('#F0F0F0')` -> `.backgroundColor(WEIGHT_PANEL_ALT_BG)`
     - `.backgroundColor('#F5F5F5')` -> `.backgroundColor(WEIGHT_PANEL_ALT_BG)`
     - border colors `#DCDCDC`, `#D1D5DB`, `#CCCCCC` -> `WEIGHT_BORDER`
   - Then patched builders:
     - `sectionStyle` bg `WEIGHT_PANEL_BG`
     - `buildCell` font color + header/body bg.
     - several common input/value builders got `.fontColor(WEIGHT_TEXT)`.
   - Need continue scanning because not all text boxes may have font color; also some replacement did not catch ternary old text until manual patch.

**OpenAI Codex**

<permissions instructions>
Filesystem sandboxing defines which files can be read or written. `sandbox_mode` is `workspace-write`: The sandbox permits reading files, and editing files in `cwd` and `writable_roots`. Editing files in other directories requires approval. Network access is restricted.
# Escalation Requests

Commands are run outside the sandbox if they are approved by the user, or match an existing rule that allows it to run unrestricted. The command string is split into independent command segments at shell control operators, including but not limited to:

- Pipes: |
- Logical operators: &&, ||
- Command separators: ;
- Subshell boundaries: (...), $(...)

Each resulting segment is evaluated independently for sandbox restrictions and approval requirements.

Example:

git pull | tee output.txt

This is treated as two command segments:

["git", "pull"]

["tee", "output.txt"]

Commands that use more advanced shell features like redirection (>, >>, <), substitutions ($(...), ...), environment variables (FOO=bar), or wildcard patterns (*, ?) will not be evaluated against rules, to limit the scope of what an approved rule allows.

## How to request escalation

IMPORTANT: To request approval to execute a command that will require escalated privileges:

- Provide the `sandbox_permissions` parameter with the value `"require_escalated"`
- Include a short question asking the user if they want to allow the action in `justification` parameter. e.g. "Do you want to download and install dependencies for this project?"
- Optionally suggest a `prefix_rule` - this will be shown to the user with an option to persist the rule approval for future sessions.

If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with "require_escalated". ALWAYS proceed to use the `justification` parameter - do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.

## When to request escalation

While commands are running inside the sandbox, here are some scenarios that will require escalation outside the sandbox:

- You need to run a command that writes to a directory that requires it (e.g. running tests that write to /var)
- You need to run a GUI app (e.g., open/xdg-open/osascript) to open browsers or files.
- If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with `require_escalated`. ALWAYS proceed to use the `sandbox_permissions` and `justification` parameters. do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.
- You are about to take a potentially destructive action such as an `rm` or `git reset` that the user did not explicitly ask for.
- Be judicious with escalating, but if completing the user's request requires it, you should do so - don't try and circumvent approvals by using other tools.

## prefix_rule guidance

When choosing a `prefix_rule`, request one that will allow you to fulfill similar requests from the user in the future without re-requesting escalation. It should be categorical and reasonably scoped to similar capabilities. You should rarely pass the entire command into `prefix_rule`.

### Banned prefix_rules 
Avoid requesting overly broad prefixes that the user would be ill-advised to approve. For example, do not request ["python3"], ["python", "-"], or other similar prefixes that would allow arbitrary scripting.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule argument for destructive commands like rm.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule if your command uses a heredoc or herestring. 

### Examples
Good examples of prefixes:
- ["npm", "run", "dev"]
- ["gh", "pr", "check"]
- ["cargo", "test"]


## Approved command prefixes
The following prefix rules have already been approved: - ["go", "test"]
- ["C:\\Program Files\\PowerShell\\7\\pwsh.exe", "-Command", "$path='E:\\new\\my_harmony\\entry\\src\\main\\ets\\utils\\network\\HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets'; $text=[System.IO.File]::ReadAllText($path); $text=$text -replace \"`r?`n\", \"`r`n\"; [System.IO.File]::WriteAllText($path, $text, [System.Text.UTF8Encoding]::new($false))"]
- ["git", "checkout-index", "--force", "--", "entry/src/main/ets/utils/network/HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets"]
- ["git", "apply", "--ignore-space-change", "--ignore-whitespace", "E:\\goTest\\tools\\frontend_grade_name_diagnostics.patch"]
 The writable root is `E:\goTest`.
</permissions instructions>

然后去看一下48里面的语言是怎么弄的 我感觉我也需要实现这个语言功能 就是多语言 的功能 然后这个用户手册的弹窗样式不一样

**OpenAI Codex**

我先去看 48 的语言切换到底是数据库配置、文件资源，还是 Qt 自己的翻译机制；同时看一下鸿蒙现在的语言入口和用户手册弹窗。先摸清，不急着乱改核心逻辑。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

48 的搜索结果很明确：它不是 Qt 自带 `.ts/.qm` 为主，而是自己有一套 `MultiLanguage`，从 `Language/<语言名>.ing` 文件读翻译，并把当前语言保存到数据库配置“选择的语言”。我再看语言切换窗口和鸿蒙现有 I18nManager。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

鸿蒙其实已经有一套 `I18nManager`，也是“语言文件 + 当前语言持久化 + AppStorage 触发刷新”的路子，只是现在入口/弹窗样式和覆盖面还不够像 48。下一步我看 48 的切换弹窗细节和你这边用户手册弹窗样式。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

还有个关键点：48 切换语言后会提示确认，然后保存“选择的语言”，最后重启程序；鸿蒙这边已经能热切换（不重启），所以没必要照搬重启。现在更需要补的是入口样式统一、手册弹窗统一，以及语言弹窗别再是那种白卡/emoji 风。

**OpenAI Codex**

我发现鸿蒙这边还有个实际问题：`EntryAbility` 里初始化 `I18nManager` 被注释掉了，`Home` 里也只有在打开语言弹窗/翻译管理时才初始化。所以如果用户之前选了 English，重启后可能不会立刻加载翻译。这个我一起补上。

**OpenAI Codex**

看完 48 了：它的语言功能是 `Language/*.ing` 文件驱动的，启动时从数据库配置 `选择的语言` 读取语言名，加载 `Language/<语言>.ing`，切换语言后保存配置并重启程序。

我这边先帮你补了鸿蒙的关键点：

- `Home.ets` 启动时初始化 `I18nManager`，这样重启后会直接加载上次选择的语言。
- 语言选择弹窗改成和更多设置一致的暗色窗口，不再是 emoji/白卡风格。
- 用户手册弹窗也统一成同一套暗色样式，标题栏、关闭按钮、列表区域都对齐了。

验证：跑了 `git diff --check`，没跑 `hvigor`。  
补一句：鸿蒙现在已经有多语言底座，后面主要是继续把残留硬编码文案接到 `t(...)`，这样语言文件才能覆盖更多界面。

---


**User**

我可以和他一样 用.ing来读取吗？ 先不要修改我的代码

---


**OpenAI Codex**

可以，用 `.ing` 来读是可以的，但我建议先别直接照搬 48 的格式，先确认 `.ing` 文件内容结构。

48 的逻辑大概是：

- 当前语言名保存在数据库配置：`tb_sys_cfg` 里的 `选择的语言`
- 启动时读这个值，比如 `English` / `Chinese`
- 然后加载：
  `应用目录/Language/English.ing`
- `MultiLanguage::GetTranslationMap(...)` 把 `.ing` 解析成一个 key-value 字典
- UI 里用类似 `MultiLanguage::GetText("xxx", langInfo)` 取文案
- 切换语言后保存 `选择的语言`，然后重启程序让所有窗口重新加载

鸿蒙这边当然也可以改成：

```text
filesDir/i18n/English.ing
filesDir/i18n/Chinese.ing
```

然后 `I18nManager` 不读 `English.json`，改成读 `.ing`。

不过要注意三个点：

1. `.ing` 不是标准格式  
   JSON 是系统天然好解析，`.ing` 是 48 自己定义的格式。鸿蒙要自己写 parser。

2. 你现在鸿蒙已经有 `I18nManager`  
   当前是读 `English.json`，`t(key, fallback)` 这套已经能用。要换 `.ing`，最好是在 `I18nManager` 里兼容 `.ing`，不要推倒重写。

3. 48 切换语言后重启，鸿蒙可以不重启  
   鸿蒙现在用 `AppStorage + I18N_VERSION_KEY` 可以热刷新 UI，这点比 48 更好，不一定要照搬重启。

我建议方案是：保留鸿蒙现有 `t(...)` 调用方式，只让 `I18nManager` 支持两种文件：

```text
优先读取 English.ing
没有 .ing 再读取 English.json
```

这样以后主管给你 48 的 `.ing` 文件，你可以直接放进去用；现在已有的 JSON 也不会废掉。

**User**

**OpenAI Codex**

对，这个思路是对的：如果 48 已经有多语言 `.ing` 文件，你最好直接复用，不要重新手写一套翻译。

更合适的做法是：

1. 把 48 的 `Language/*.ing` 拷到鸿蒙资源里  
   比如放到 `rawfile/language/English.ing`、`Chinese.ing`、`Spanish.ing` 之类。

2. 鸿蒙启动时复制到沙盒  
   类似你用户手册那套逻辑，把资源文件复制到 `filesDir/i18n/`。

3. 改 `I18nManager` 支持读取 `.ing`  
   保持现有 `t('中文key', '中文key')` 不变，只是底层从 `.ing` 文件拿翻译。

4. 当前语言仍然用鸿蒙自己的持久化保存  
   不一定要完全照 48 存 `tb_sys_cfg.选择的语言`，除非你希望前后端/设备也知道当前语言。UI 自己用的话存在 Preferences 就够了。

唯一要确认的是：48 的 `.ing` 里面 key 是什么。  
如果 key 是类似：

```text
Save=保存
Cancel=取消
RSS.OptionForm=...
```

那鸿蒙现有 `t('保存', '保存')` 这种中文 key 可能匹配不上，需要做一层映射。  
如果 `.ing` 里也包含中文原文作为 key，那就很舒服，能直接用。

所以下一步不是写翻译，而是先打开 48 的 `.ing` 看格式和 key。确认格式后，就可以做一个 `.ing` parser，把 48 的语言包接进鸿蒙。

**User**

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我看一下你贴的这个 `.ing` 内容结构，确认它是 XML 资源格式还是简单 key-value。这个会决定鸿蒙这边 parser 怎么接。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

是的，这个 `.ing` 本质上是 **XML 格式语言包**，不是普通 key=value。

结构是这样的：

```xml
<Resources>
  <RSS.AboutForm Title="">
    <label4 Tip="">Module compile date</label4>
    <uiGroupBox1 Tip="">HC Infomation</uiGroupBox1>
  </RSS.AboutForm>
</Resources>
```

也就是说翻译 key 其实可以理解成：

```text
RSS.AboutForm.label4 = Module compile date
RSS.AboutForm.uiGroupBox1 = HC Infomation
```

`Tip=""` 是提示文本/备注属性，真正显示文本是标签中间的内容。

所以鸿蒙可以复用这个 `.ing`，但有个关键点：你现在鸿蒙很多地方是这样写的：

```ts
t('用户手册', '用户手册')
t('打印设置', '打印设置')
```

而 48 的 `.ing` key 是：

```text
RSS.AboutForm.label4
RSS.DownConfigForm.btn_Down
RSS.DeviceInfoForm.label1
```

这两个体系不一样，所以不能“直接丢进去就全部生效”。

我建议做法是：

1. `I18nManager` 支持读取 `.ing`
2. 解析成 `Map<string, string>`
3. key 用 `父节点名.子节点名`
   例如：`RSS.AboutForm.label4`
4. 后面鸿蒙对应 48 的页面，逐步改成：
   ```ts
   t('RSS.AboutForm.label4', '模块编译日期')
   ```
5. 这样 48 已有的英文、西班牙文等 `.ing` 可以直接复用

这样最稳。不是重新写翻译，而是把鸿蒙的显示 key 对齐 48 的语言包 key。

**OpenAI Codex**

没翻译到位的处理方式，我建议这样分：

1. 不建议直接改 48 原始 `.ing`
   因为以后如果又从 48 同步新版语言包，你手改的内容会被覆盖。

2. 如果是鸿蒙新增文案，48 没有对应 key  
   最好做一个鸿蒙自己的补丁语言文件，例如：
   `Harmony.English.json` 或继续用现有 `English.json`，优先级高于 `.ing`。
   这样 48 的包保持原样，鸿蒙缺的自己补。

3. 如果是 48 有翻译但鸿蒙没匹配上  
   那就把鸿蒙里的 `t('中文', '中文')` 改成 48 的 key：
   ```ts
   t('RSS.ConfigSetForm.FTypeCol', '配置名称')
   ```
   这种最稳，直接复用 48 的已有翻译。

我建议后面按第 3 种优先：看到哪个没翻译，就找 48 `.ing` 对应 key，把鸿蒙那句 `t(...)` 改成 48 key。找不到再走第 2 种补丁。

**OpenAI Codex**

<permissions instructions>
Filesystem sandboxing defines which files can be read or written. `sandbox_mode` is `workspace-write`: The sandbox permits reading files, and editing files in `cwd` and `writable_roots`. Editing files in other directories requires approval. Network access is restricted.
# Escalation Requests

Commands are run outside the sandbox if they are approved by the user, or match an existing rule that allows it to run unrestricted. The command string is split into independent command segments at shell control operators, including but not limited to:

- Pipes: |
- Logical operators: &&, ||
- Command separators: ;
- Subshell boundaries: (...), $(...)

Each resulting segment is evaluated independently for sandbox restrictions and approval requirements.

Example:

git pull | tee output.txt

This is treated as two command segments:

["git", "pull"]

["tee", "output.txt"]

Commands that use more advanced shell features like redirection (>, >>, <), substitutions ($(...), ...), environment variables (FOO=bar), or wildcard patterns (*, ?) will not be evaluated against rules, to limit the scope of what an approved rule allows.

## How to request escalation

IMPORTANT: To request approval to execute a command that will require escalated privileges:

- Provide the `sandbox_permissions` parameter with the value `"require_escalated"`
- Include a short question asking the user if they want to allow the action in `justification` parameter. e.g. "Do you want to download and install dependencies for this project?"
- Optionally suggest a `prefix_rule` - this will be shown to the user with an option to persist the rule approval for future sessions.

If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with "require_escalated". ALWAYS proceed to use the `justification` parameter - do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.

## When to request escalation

While commands are running inside the sandbox, here are some scenarios that will require escalation outside the sandbox:

- You need to run a command that writes to a directory that requires it (e.g. running tests that write to /var)
- You need to run a GUI app (e.g., open/xdg-open/osascript) to open browsers or files.
- If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with `require_escalated`. ALWAYS proceed to use the `sandbox_permissions` and `justification` parameters. do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.
- You are about to take a potentially destructive action such as an `rm` or `git reset` that the user did not explicitly ask for.
- Be judicious with escalating, but if completing the user's request requires it, you should do so - don't try and circumvent approvals by using other tools.

## prefix_rule guidance

When choosing a `prefix_rule`, request one that will allow you to fulfill similar requests from the user in the future without re-requesting escalation. It should be categorical and reasonably scoped to similar capabilities. You should rarely pass the entire command into `prefix_rule`.

### Banned prefix_rules 
Avoid requesting overly broad prefixes that the user would be ill-advised to approve. For example, do not request ["python3"], ["python", "-"], or other similar prefixes that would allow arbitrary scripting.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule argument for destructive commands like rm.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule if your command uses a heredoc or herestring. 

### Examples
Good examples of prefixes:
- ["npm", "run", "dev"]
- ["gh", "pr", "check"]
- ["cargo", "test"]


## Approved command prefixes
The following prefix rules have already been approved: - ["go", "test"]
- ["Get-Content", "-LiteralPath", "E:\\new\\my_harmony\\entry\\src\\main\\ets\\pages\\Home.ets"]
- ["Get-Content", "-LiteralPath", "E:\\new\\my_harmony\\entry\\src\\main\\ets\\components\\dialogs\\ElectricalFaultDialog.ets"]
- ["Get-Content", "-LiteralPath", "E:\\new\\my_harmony\\entry\\src\\main\\ets\\components\\dialogs\\pages\\WeightSettingsPage.ets"]
- ["C:\\Program Files\\PowerShell\\7\\pwsh.exe", "-Command", "Select-String -LiteralPath 'E:\\new\\my_harmony\\entry\\src\\main\\ets\\components\\dialogs\\pages\\WeightSettingsPage.ets' -Pattern \"算法 1|算法 2|平均重量|G-AD系数|Text\\(option|Select\\(this.getChannelOptions\" -Context 0,5"]
- ["C:\\Program Files\\PowerShell\\7\\pwsh.exe", "-Command", "$path='E:\\new\\my_harmony\\entry\\src\\main\\ets\\utils\\network\\HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets'; $text=[System.IO.File]::ReadAllText($path); $text=$text -replace \"`r?`n\", \"`r`n\"; [System.IO.File]::WriteAllText($path, $text, [System.Text.UTF8Encoding]::new($false))"]
- ["git", "checkout-index", "--force", "--", "entry/src/main/ets/utils/network/HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets"]
- ["git", "apply", "--ignore-space-change", "--ignore-whitespace", "E:\\goTest\\tools\\frontend_grade_name_diagnostics.patch"]
- ["git", "-C", "E:\\new\\my_harmony", "diff", "--", "entry/src/main/ets/pages/Home.ets"]
- ["git", "-C", "E:\\new\\my_harmony", "diff", "--check", "--", "entry/src/main/ets/pages/Home.ets", "entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/ResetCupConfirmDialog.ets", "entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/TestCupDialog.ets"]
 The writable root is `E:\goTest`.
</permissions instructions>

**OpenAI Codex**

关键点找到了：首页波浪高度不是看第三层绑定数据，而是看 `EXIT_PERCENT_出口号` 这组运行态缓存；`clearAllCardData()` 只清了第三层列表，没有清 `EXIT_PERCENT_/EXIT_WEIGHT_/EXIT_COUNT_`。所以界面会残留上一批波浪值。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我不会直接调用 `gdi.clearData()` 来偷懒，因为它会把加工状态、开始时间也清掉，风险太大。这里应该只清首页出口运行态缓存：数量、重量、百分比，再触发 `EXIT_RUNTIME_VERSION`，让卡片自己刷新波浪。

**OpenAI Codex**

准备改两个点：`LiquidCardsArea` 增加一个“只清出口运行态缓存”的方法；`数据清零` 成功后调用它。`出口清空` 会顺便清同一组运行态缓存，这样波浪图不会等拖拽才变。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

`出口清空` 这边已经补上了运行态缓存清零。接下来把 `数据清零` 的成功路径接到同一个刷新方法，但不会清出口绑定。

**OpenAI Codex**

修改点很小：`数据清零` 现在只清首页出口运行态缓存；`出口清空` 则在清绑定数据时一起清波浪运行态。现在做静态检查和针对性脚本检查，不编译。

已有的出口清空保护脚本通过了；另一个兼容脚本挂在 `LevelContent.ets` 的旧断言上，和这次清波浪图改动无关。我再做一个针对这次链路的快速检查，确认两个入口都接到了清运行态。

**OpenAI Codex**

改好了。问题根因是：波浪图读的是 `EXIT_PERCENT_出口号` 这类运行态缓存，并靠 `EXIT_RUNTIME_VERSION` 刷新；之前样式改完后，确认按钮只是发了清空命令，`数据清零` 没清本地运行态，`出口清空` 也只清了第三层/出口绑定数据，所以波浪图残留，拖拽后才被动刷新。

- [LiquidCardsArea.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/pages/home/LiquidCardsArea.ets:276)：新增清空 `EXIT_COUNT_ / EXIT_WEIGHT_ / EXIT_PERCENT_` 并递增 `EXIT_RUNTIME_VERSION` 的逻辑；`出口清空` 会一起清波浪运行态。
- [Home.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/pages/Home.ets:2205)：`数据清零` 发送成功后，只清首页出口运行态，不清出口绑定关系。

**OpenAI Codex**

现在我要看实时数据同步层：谁在持续写 `EXIT_PERCENT_`，以及它有没有清零保护。现在的异常基本就是“旧统计帧回写”造成的，但要在代码里确认写入口。

**OpenAI Codex**

确认了，`UIDataSync` 每秒也会主动同步一次，所以即使你刚点完清零，本地波浪先归零，1 秒内仍可能被它从旧的 `GlobalDataInterface` 快照写回去。根因不是弹窗，是清零后的旧实时快照没有被同步层认出来。

**OpenAI Codex**

现在的修复方向：清零后设置一个很短的“出口清零保护窗口”。在这个窗口内，`UIDataSync` 如果还读到旧的非零出口统计，就继续向 UI 写 0；等读到真正全 0 或超时，就退出保护。这样不会出现“清了又回去”的闪烁。

**OpenAI Codex**

**OpenAI Codex**

断言按预期失败了：同步层没有清零保护。现在补到 `UIDataSync`，并让 `数据清零/出口清空` 成功后启用它。
